 At a time when there are protests in the country over the Land Acquisition Act and the debate on the coal bill is hot, the government is trying to pass the Mines and Minerals (regulation) Amendment Bill related to the country's natural wealth and resources
 ise mins and mineral (deveopment and regulation  amendament) bill bhi kaha jaataa he
 If you look closely, this bill has more loopholes than the other two proposed bills
 
 
 abhi is par sansad kii select cameti bahes kar rahi he
 According to sources, many members of the committee have objected to many points of the bill and the passage of this bill in the Rajya Sabha is not easy unless it is done with heavy amendments
 enditivi india ne is kanoon kaa dhyaan se adhyayan kiya or is par jaankaron se baat kii, jisase pataa chalata he ki is kanoon ke banane ke baad bhi sarkaar ke tamaam khanij bhandaron ke nilaamee ke daawey dhare rah jaaenge
 Let us first understand what this bill is
 bharat main 1957 se chale aa rahe kanoon ko badalane ke liye saal 2010 main ek nae kanoon kaa prastaav aayaa, lekin vah prastaav 2014 tak kanoon nahin ban sakaa
 The new government has introduced amendments to the old law of 1957 in place of that new bill
 ye sanshodhan aise badlaav hai jo kisi had tak mining bill ko kamazor karte hai
 With the introduction of this bill according to the government, the allocation of mines of iron ore, bauxite, lime stone and manganese will be on auction basis
 sarkaar yah bhi bataa rahi he ki is kanoon ke ban jane ke baad baaki khanijon kii nilaamee se vaisaa hi phayda hoga, jaisaa koyala khadaanon kii tazaa nilaamee se hua he
 If you read the bill, para 10 of the amendment bill for it
 e
 1 says that after the enactment of this law, all the old applications related to mining will be canceled
 lekin isi bill ke agle para main kaha gaya he ki jin companiyon ko khojbin or survey ke liye ijazat (riconicense permit) or procepective license (yani kaam shuru karne kaa license) de di gai he, ve bane rahenge
 Today the reality is that more than 80 percent of the known mineral deposits in the country have been given investigative surveys or prospecting licenses
 aise main sawaal yah he ki nayaa kanoon kis kaam kaa hoga
 Sudeep Srivastava, a lawyer and mining expert who was a petitioner in the coal case, says, "now much money is being received in the coal block auction because the Supreme Court canceled all 214 coal blocks, but this mining bill does not cancel the old mineral deposits
" But rather legalizes them
 ' Srivastava says that almost all known mineral deposits in the country have been given through a survey or prospective license, which this new law will not repeal
 vah chhattisgarh kaa udhaaharan dete hue kehete hai, 'chhattisgarh main kaverdha louh ayask ke bhandar ko chhod den to baaki khadaanon kii yaa to mining leez ho chuki he yaa companiyon ke paas unka prospective license he
 In such a situation, what will this law do? saaf he ki is kanoon ke aane ke baad ek ore jahaan badi sankhya main khanij bhandaron kii nilaamee nahin ho paaegi, vahiin ye vidheyak chaalu khadaanon kii leez kii miyaad ko bhi ek jatke main 30 saal se badhaakar 50 saal kar rahaa he
 Right now, the increase in the period rests with the state governments, where they decide according to the benefit of the state

 notebandi par jari siyaasi ghamaasan ke bich sarkaar ab plastic ke note laane kii taiyaari main he
 Minister of State for Finance Arjun Ram Meghwal gave this information in Parliament on Friday
 unhone bataaya ki ab plastic kii karency chhaapi jaaegi, iske liye kaccha maal kharida ja he
 The Reserve Bank of India has been planning to launch plastic currency for quite some time
 farvari 2014 main sarkaar ne sansad ko jaankaree di thi ki 10 rupee vaale ek arbaplastic notchape jaaenge or inke field trial ke liye 5 shahar chune gaye hai
 These cities were Kochi, Mysore, Jaipur, Shimla and Bhubaneswar
 kaise hote hai plastic ke note, kya he inaki khaasiyatplastic se bane karency note paper vaale noton kii tulana main saaf-suthere hote hai
 These are also called polymer notes
 plastic ke noton kii ausat umr kareeb paanch saal hoti he
 That is, more than double the notes of paper
 plastic noton kii nakal utaarna aasaan nahin hota he
 According to one study, plastic notes reduce global warming by 32% and energy demand by 30% as compared to paper notes
 plastic vaale noton kaa vajan paper vaale noton kii tulana main kam hota he
 In such a situation, their transportation and distribution is also easy
 kaagaj vaale puraane noton ko nasht karne ke liye jalaana padataa he jabaki plastic vaale noton ko ricycle kar chharre banaae jate hai yaa phir inhen plastic kii duusari chijen banaai ja sakati hai
 The practice of such notes first began in Australia

 Sarabjit Singh, imprisoned in Pakistan, is neither to be released nor his sentence has been reduced
 pakistan ke raashtrapati karyaalay ke pravaktaa farhatulla babar ne bataaya he ki jis vyakti kii rihaai kii baat kii gai he, uskaa naam surajeet singh he
 Earlier on Tuesday evening, there was news that President Asif Ali Zardari had waived the death sentence of Sarabjit Singh, an Indian citizen who has been jailed for the last 22 years in Pakistan and his sentence has been commuted to life imprisonment
 iske baad kayaas lagaae ja rahe the ki sarbajit ko kabhi bhi reeha kiya ja saktaa he, lekin der shaam pakistan ke raashtrapati karyaalay ke pravaktaa ne is baat kii pushti kii ki sarbajit singh kii rihaai nahin hogi, balki surajeet singh kii rihaai kaa faisla liya gaya he
 People of his family are very angry with the news of Sarabjit Singh's release being false
 unki bahan dalbir cor kaa kahana he ki unako is khabar se dhakka laga he or unki bhaawanaaon ke saath bhi khilwaad kiya gaya he
 However, Dalbir has also said that he has full faith in Pakistan President Asif Ali Zardari that he will release Sarabjit as soon as possible
 sarbajit ko 1990 main pakistan ke shahar lahore or faisalabad main hue chaar bam dhamaakon ke aarope main giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 10 people were killed in these blasts
 us vakt sarbajit ko manajit singh ke naam se giraftaar kiya gaya tha
 After being arrested, Sarabjit had said that he had no hand in these bombings and was a resident of Tarn Taran in Punjab province of India and had accidentally crossed the border to Pakistan
 iske baad sarbajit par jasusi or bam dhamaakon ke aarope main lahore kii ek adaalat main mukadmaa chalaa or 1991 main unhen maut kii sajaa sunai gai
 This sentence of the lower court was upheld by the High Court and also by the Supreme Court
 tippaniyan Surjit Singh, whose release has been reported by Pakistan President's Office spokesman Farhatullah Babar, was arrested in 1982 on espionage charges in Pakistan
 1985 main army kii court ne surajeet ko faansee kii sajaa sunai thi
 After this, Surjit's death sentence was changed to life imprisonment by Pakistani President Ishaq Khan in 1988
 2010 main surajeet ne apni sajaa puri kii, lekin unki rihaai nahin hui
 Subsequently Surjeet's case reached Lahore Court from where orders were given to release him as soon as possible
 isse pehle mangalvaar shaam ko khabar ai thi ki pakistan main pichley 22 saal se jail main band bhartiya naagarik sarbajit singh kii faansee kii sajaa ko raashtrapati asif ali jaradaari ne maaf kar diya he or unki sajaa ko umrakaid main badal diya gaya he
 After this there were speculations that Sarabjit could be released at any time, but late in the evening, a spokesman of the President's Office of Pakistan confirmed that there would be no release of Sarabjit Singh, but decided to release Surjit Singh

 in dhamaakon main 10 logon kii maut ho gai thi

 lagbhag 30 karod log apni aajeevika ke liye vyapaariyon par nirbhar hai
 The country has an annual turnover of about 42 lakh crores, with a growth rate of about 10 percent per annum, it is a matter of great regret that since independence, the Congress Government has never made any effort to develop domestic business in a planned manner and It was always tried that Indian traders should depend on the goods imported from abroad

 1
 5 din ke bheetar upi main doosraa rail haadasa, danpar se takaraai kiafiyat express, 10 dibbe patari se utre, 21 ghayalupi main ek or rail haadasa hua he

 azamgarh se dilli aa rahi 12225 (ap) kiafiyat express auraiya ke paas durghatnagrast ho gai
 Late night at the unmanned gate, the train collided with a dumper
